        </expr>
        <expr line1="61" col1="3" line2="61" col2="6" start="7811" end="7814">

  <COMMENT line1="64" col1="1" line2="64" col2="39" start="8193" end="8231">#' DESeqDataSet object and constructors</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="65" col1="1" line2="65" col2="2" start="8321" end="8322">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="66" col1="1" line2="66" col2="74" start="8449" end="8522">#' \code{DESeqDataSet} is a subclass of \code{RangedSummarizedExperiment},</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="67" col1="1" line2="67" col2="78" start="8577" end="8654">#' used to store the input values, intermediate calculations and results of an</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="68" col1="1" line2="68" col2="70" start="8705" end="8774">#' analysis of differential expression.  The \code{DESeqDataSet} class</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="69" col1="1" line2="69" col2="72" start="8833" end="8904">#' enforces non-negative integer values in the "counts" matrix stored as</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="70" col1="1" line2="70" col2="39" start="8961" end="8999">#' the first element in the assay list.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="71" col1="1" line2="71" col2="88" start="9089" end="9176">#' In addition, a formula which specifies the design of the experiment must be provided.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="72" col1="1" line2="72" col2="57" start="9217" end="9273">#' The constructor functions create a DESeqDataSet object</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="73" col1="1" line2="73" col2="31" start="9345" end="9375">#' from various types of input:</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="74" col1="1" line2="74" col2="67" start="9473" end="9539">#' a RangedSummarizedExperiment, a matrix, count files generated by</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="75" col1="1" line2="75" col2="72" start="9601" end="9672">#' the python package HTSeq, or a list from the tximport function in the</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="76" col1="1" line2="76" col2="20" start="9729" end="9748">#' tximport package.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="77" col1="1" line2="77" col2="70" start="9857" end="9926">#' See the vignette for examples of construction from different types.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="78" col1="1" line2="78" col2="2" start="9985" end="9986">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="79" col1="1" line2="79" col2="89" start="10113" end="10201">#' Note on the error message "assay colnames() must be NULL or equal colData rownames()":</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="80" col1="1" line2="80" col2="88" start="10241" end="10328">#' this means that the colnames of countData are different than the rownames of colData.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="81" col1="1" line2="81" col2="52" start="10369" end="10420">#' Fix this with: \code{colnames(countData) &lt;- NULL}</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="82" col1="1" line2="82" col2="2" start="10497" end="10498">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="83" col1="1" line2="83" col2="74" start="10625" end="10698">#' @param se a \code{RangedSummarizedExperiment} with columns of variables</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="84" col1="1" line2="84" col2="51" start="10753" end="10803">#' indicating sample information in \code{colData},</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="85" col1="1" line2="85" col2="69" start="10881" end="10949">#' and the counts as the first element in the assays list, which will</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="86" col1="1" line2="86" col2="73" start="11009" end="11081">#' be renamed "counts". A \code{RangedSummarizedExperiment} object can be</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="87" col1="1" line2="87" col2="78" start="11137" end="11214">#' generated by the function \code{summarizeOverlaps} in the GenomicAlignments</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="88" col1="1" line2="88" col2="11" start="11265" end="11275">#' package.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="89" col1="1" line2="89" col2="51" start="11393" end="11443">#' @param design a \code{formula} or \code{matrix}.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="90" col1="1" line2="90" col2="60" start="11521" end="11580">#' the \code{formula} expresses how the counts for each gene</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="91" col1="1" line2="91" col2="78" start="11649" end="11726">#' depend on the variables in \code{colData}. Many R \code{formula} are valid,</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="92" col1="1" line2="92" col2="79" start="11777" end="11855">#' including designs with multiple variables, e.g., \code{~ group + condition},</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="93" col1="1" line2="93" col2="91" start="11905" end="11995">#' and designs with interactions, e.g., \code{~ genotype + treatment + genotype:treatment}.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="94" col1="1" line2="94" col2="88" start="12033" end="12120">#' See \code{\link{results}} for a variety of designs and how to extract results tables.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="95" col1="1" line2="95" col2="54" start="12161" end="12214">#' By default, the functions in this package will use </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="96" col1="1" line2="96" col2="77" start="12289" end="12365">#' the last variable in the formula for building results tables and plotting.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="97" col1="1" line2="97" col2="72" start="12417" end="12488">#' \code{~ 1} can be used for no design, although users need to remember</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="98" col1="1" line2="98" col2="56" start="12545" end="12600">#' to switch to another design for differential testing.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="99" col1="1" line2="99" col2="71" start="12673" end="12743">#' @param countData for matrix input: a matrix of non-negative integers</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="100" col1="1" line2="100" col2="106" start="12801" end="12906">#' @param colData for matrix input: a \code{DataFrame} or \code{data.frame} with at least a single column.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="101" col1="1" line2="101" col2="53" start="12929" end="12981">#' Rows of colData correspond to columns of countData</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="102" col1="1" line2="102" col2="107" start="13057" end="13163">#' @param tidy for matrix input: whether the first column of countData is the rownames for the count matrix</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="103" col1="1" line2="103" col2="95" start="13185" end="13279">#' @param sampleTable for htseq-count: a \code{data.frame} with three or more columns. Each row</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="104" col1="1" line2="104" col2="79" start="13313" end="13391">#' describes one sample. The first column is the sample name, the second column</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="105" col1="1" line2="105" col2="78" start="13441" end="13518">#' the file name of the count file generated by htseq-count, and the remaining</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="106" col1="1" line2="106" col2="69" start="13569" end="13637">#' columns are sample metadata which will be stored in \code{colData}</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="107" col1="1" line2="107" col2="82" start="13697" end="13778">#' @param txi for tximport: the simple list output of the \code{tximport} function</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="109" col1="1" line2="109" col2="81" start="13953" end="14033">#' @param ignoreRank use of this argument is reserved for DEXSeq developers only.</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="111" col1="1" line2="111" col2="61" start="14209" end="14269">#' using a design with a model matrix which is not full rank.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="112" col1="1" line2="112" col2="107" start="14337" end="14443">#' @param ... arguments provided to \code{SummarizedExperiment} including rowRanges and metadata. Note that</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="113" col1="1" line2="113" col2="100" start="14465" end="14564">#' for Bioconductor 3.1, rowRanges must be a GRanges or GRangesList, with potential metadata columns</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="114" col1="1" line2="114" col2="98" start="14593" end="14690">#' as a DataFrame accessed and stored with \code{mcols}. If a user wants to store metadata columns</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="116" col1="1" line2="116" col2="104" start="14849" end="14952">#' first construct the DESeqDataSet without rowRanges and then add the DataFrame with \code{mcols(dds)}.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="117" col1="1" line2="117" col2="3" start="14977" end="14979">#' </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="118" col1="1" line2="118" col2="33" start="15105" end="15137">#' @return A DESeqDataSet object.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="119" col1="1" line2="119" col2="3" start="15233" end="15235">#' </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="120" col1="1" line2="120" col2="93" start="15361" end="15453">#' @aliases DESeqDataSet DESeqDataSet-class DESeqDataSetFromMatrix DESeqDataSetFromHTSeqCount</COMMENT>
